name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 3, 2023
msg:As soon as you enter the hotel, someone will come out to greet you and help you with your luggage, and you can also take the initiative to store your luggage. However, there happens to be a wedding package hall on October 1st that day, so you can't eat in the hall. The receptionist said that meals can be delivered to the room, but you have to A 15% service fee is charged. Due to special circumstances, the service fee is reduced. The portion of the dish is relatively large, and I think the taste is okay. The mushroom meatball soup in the evening is worth recommending, it is very delicious. At that time, I really wanted to drink porridge at night, so I ordered a bowl of pumpkin and millet porridge for 5 yuan, which I thought was okay. The specialty called fried crunchy mung bean noodles was too sweet, like Beijing's sweet and sour pork loin, so I don't recommend it. Next to the hotel is the scenic spot Shuangta Mountain, which is a 5-minute walk away. Well, you can also watch macaques when you climb up the mountain, which feels a bit captive. We drove to the hotel from Beijing, so it took less than 30 minutes to drive from the hotel to Chengde Summer Resort and the Little Potala Palace on the second day. It felt quite convenient. What the hotel said was Butler-style management responds quickly to your service requests. The decoration of solid wood facilities throughout the hotel is its characteristic, and you can take a good walk around the hotel. But the only regret is that the morning buffet is rich in variety and delicious, but there are relatively few seats. Fortunately, we found a seat on the terrace. The sun hit the terrace at eight or nine o'clock on October 2nd, and it wasn't very hot or cold. You could also see the Twin Towers Mountain from the terrace, so I thought it was okay. In short, I am quite satisfied with the hotel's facilities and services and the price-performance ratio is quite high. I hope to keep up the good work.

msg:The hotel service was very satisfactory and there were no issues during our stay.
The hotel is indeed as the name suggests, and it does feel like you are walking through a palace, but the height issue makes it a little depressing.
The rooms are all made of Chinese wooden furniture, without any smell. The hotel decoration design is also very tasteful, and it is very comfortable to stay.
The hotel is right in front of Shuangta Mountain, so it's very convenient to just stroll there. At night, Shuangtashan Square is very lively with various children's entertainment projects and various small vendors. Many residents come to enjoy the cool air. It is also good to experience the local nightlife.
The final suggestion is that the breakfast ends a bit early. It would be better if it can be served at 10 o'clock. I will come here again when passing through Chengde in the future.
